Source Code

These source code files are a reconstruction of Sundance, the Apollo 9 LM (Lunar Module) AGC (Apollo Guidance Computer) flight software, created from binary dumps of original core rope program modules, as follows:
  • B1 — Revision 292
  • B2 — Revision 302
  • B3 — Revision 302
  • B4 — Revision 302
  • B5 — Revision 292
  • B6 — Revision 306
This means that source code does not represent a specific historical revision of Sundance, but rather a mixture of the three released versions. Nonetheless, it is capable of flying the whole Apollo 9 mission. This source code matches the binary dumps, as closely as feasible, but 100% match is not possible, due mostly to changes in memory addresses at which code and variables were allocated in different revisions of Sundance. Refer to this list of explanations for each binary mismatch.

Since only binary dumps (rather than listings) of Sundance are available as source material, all comments and labels are approximate. They have been taken from other AGC programs where possible, or, in some places, written from scratch to match what we believe would have been in the original listing. 

019631,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
019632,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
019633,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of a reconstructed, mixed version of Sundance
019634,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the Lunar
019635,000006:                                                                                                  ##              Module's (LM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 9.
019636,000007:                                                                                                  ##              No original listings of this program are available;
019637,000008:                                                                                                  ##              instead, this file was created via disassembly of dumps
019638,000009:                                                                                                  ##              of various revisions of Sundance core rope modules.
019639,000010:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
019640,000011:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
019641,000012:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
019642,000013:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2020-06-17 MAS  Created from Luminary 69.
019643,000014: 
019644,000015:                                                                                                  ## Sundance 302
019645,000016: 
019646,000017:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
019647,000018:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
019648,000019:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
019649,000020:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
019650,000021:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
019651,000022: 
019652,000023:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
019653,000024:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
019654,000025:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
019655,000026:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
019656,000027:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
019657,000028: 
019658,000029:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
019659,000030:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
019660,000031:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
019661,000032:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
019662,000033:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
019663,000034:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
019664,000035:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
019665,000036:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
019666,000037:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
019667,000038:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
019668,000039:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
019669,000040:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
019670,000041:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
019671,000042:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
019672,000043:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
019673,000044:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
019674,000045:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
019675,000046:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
019676,000047:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
019677,000048:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
019678,000049:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
019679,000050:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
019680,000051:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
019681,000052:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
019682,000053: 25,2053  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
019683,000054: 
019684,000055: 33,2000                                           BANK     33                                    
019685,000056: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
019686,000057: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
019687,000058: 
019688,000059: 24,2000  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
019689,000060: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

019971,000342:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
019972,000343:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
019973,000344:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
019974,000345:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
019975,000346:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
019976,000347: 
019977,000348:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
019978,000349:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
019979,000350:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
019980,000351:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
019981,000352:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
019982,000353:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
019983,000354:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
019984,000355:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
019985,000356:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
019986,000357:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
019987,000358:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
019988,000359:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
019989,000360:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
019990,000361:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
019991,000362:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
019992,000363:                                                                                                  #    NONE
019993,000364:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
019994,000365:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
019995,000366:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
019996,000367:                                                                                                  #    TRACKFLG,P25FLAG
019997,000368:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
019998,000369:                                                                                                  #    NONE

020057,000428:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
020058,000429:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020059,000430:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020060,000431:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
020061,000432:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020062,000433: 
020063,000434:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
020064,000435:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
020065,000436:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020066,000437:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
020067,000438:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
020068,000439:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
020069,000440:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
020070,000441:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
020071,000442:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
020072,000443:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
020073,000444:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
020074,000445:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
020075,000446:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
020076,000447:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020077,000448:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
020078,000449:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
020079,000450:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020080,000451:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
020081,000452:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020082,000453:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
020083,000454:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020084,000455:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
020085,000456:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020086,000457:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3

020255,000626:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
020256,000627:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020257,000628:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020258,000629:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
020259,000630:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020260,000631: 
020261,000632:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
020262,000633:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
020263,000634:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020264,000635:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL

020272,000643:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ

020426,000797:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
020427,000798:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020428,000799:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
020429,000800:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
020430,000801:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020431,000802: 
020432,000803:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
020433,000804:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
020434,000805:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
020435,000806:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
020436,000807:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
020437,000808:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
020438,000809:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
020439,000810:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
020440,000811:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020441,000812:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
020442,000813:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
020443,000814:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
020444,000815:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
020445,000816:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
020446,000817:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
020447,000818:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
020448,000819:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
020449,000820:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
020450,000821:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
020451,000822:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
020452,000823:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020453,000824:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
020454,000825:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET

020517,000888:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
020518,000889:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION

020523,000894:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
020524,000895:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
020525,000896:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
020526,000897:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.

020699,001070:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020700,001071:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
020701,001072:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
020702,001073:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
020703,001074:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
020704,001075:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
020705,001076:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
020706,001077:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
020707,001078:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
020708,001079:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
020709,001080:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
020710,001081:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
020711,001082:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
020712,001083:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
020713,001084:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
020714,001085:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.

020716,001087:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
020717,001088:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
020718,001089:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL

Sundance 302 

020788,001159: 
020789,001160:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
020790,001161: 
020791,001162:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020792,001163: 
020793,001164:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
020794,001165:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
020795,001166:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
020796,001167:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
020797,001168:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
020798,001169:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
020799,001170:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
020800,001171:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
020801,001172:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
020802,001173:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
020803,001174:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
020804,001175:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
020805,001176: 
020806,001177:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
020807,001178:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
020808,001179:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
020809,001180: 
020810,001181:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020811,001182:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
020812,001183: 
020813,001184:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
020814,001185: 
020815,001186:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
020816,001187:                                                                                                  #  NONE
020817,001188: 
020818,001189:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
020819,001190: 
020820,001191:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
020821,001192: 
020822,001193: 24,3116                                           BANK     24                                    
020823,001194: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
020824,001195: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
020825,001196: 
020826,001197: 25,2053  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
020827,001198: 25,2053                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
020828,001199: 25,2053           02062        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB                              
020829,001200: 25,2054           05271                           TC       FIXDELAY                              #  WAIT 1 SEC BEFORE REMOVING TURN ON FLAG
020830,001201: 25,2055           00144                           DEC      100        B-14                       #  SO A MONITOR REPOSITION WONT ALARM.
020831,001202: 25,2056           45026                           CS       BIT1                                  
020832,001203: 25,2057           71101                           MASK     RADMODES                              
020833,001204: 25,2060           55101                           TS       RADMODES                              
020834,001205: 25,2061           15321                           TCF      TASKOVER                              
020835,001206: 
020836,001207:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
020837,001208: 
020838,001209:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020839,001210:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
020840,001211:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
020841,001212:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
020842,001213:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
020843,001214:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
020844,001215:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
020845,001216:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
020846,001217:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
020847,001218:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
020848,001219:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
020849,001220:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
020850,001221:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
020851,001222:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
020852,001223:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
020853,001224:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
020854,001225: 
020855,001226:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
020856,001227:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020857,001228:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
020858,001229: 
020859,001230:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
020860,001231: 
020861,001232:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
020862,001233:                                                                                                  #  NONE
020863,001234: 
020864,001235:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
020865,001236:

020907,001278: 
020908,001279:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
020909,001280:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
020910,001281:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
020911,001282:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
020912,001283:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
020913,001284:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
020914,001285:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
020915,001286:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
020916,001287:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
020917,001288:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
020918,001289:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
020919,001290:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
020920,001291:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
020921,001292:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
020922,001293:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
020923,001294:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
020924,001295:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
020925,001296:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
020926,001297:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
020927,001298:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
020928,001299:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
020929,001300:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
020930,001301:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
020931,001302:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
020932,001303: 
020933,001304:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
020934,001305:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
020935,001306:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
020936,001307: 
020937,001308:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
020938,001309:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES

020995,001366:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                   IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
020996,001367: 
020997,001368:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
020998,001369:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
020999,001370:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
021000,001371:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
021001,001372:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
021002,001373:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
021003,001374:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
021004,001375:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021005,001376:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
021006,001377:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
021007,001378:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
021008,001379:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
021009,001380:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
021010,001381:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
021011,001382:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
021012,001383:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
021013,001384:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
021014,001385:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
021015,001386:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
021016,001387:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
021017,001388: 
021018,001389:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021019,001390:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
021020,001391:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
021021,001392:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
021022,001393:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.

021075,001446:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
021076,001447: 
021077,001448:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021078,001449:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
021079,001450:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
021080,001451:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
021081,001452:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
021082,001453:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
021083,001454:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
021084,001455:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
021085,001456:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
021086,001457:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
021087,001458:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
021088,001459:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
021089,001460:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
021090,001461:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
021091,001462:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
021092,001463: 
021093,001464:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE* (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
021094,001465:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
021095,001466:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
021096,001467:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
021097,001468:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
021098,001469: 
021099,001470:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021100,001471:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES

021161,001532: 
021162,001533:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                    RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
021163,001534: 
021164,001535:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021165,001536:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
021166,001537:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
021167,001538:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
021168,001539:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
021169,001540:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
021170,001541:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
021171,001542:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
021172,001543:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
021173,001544:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
021174,001545:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
021175,001546:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
021176,001547:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
021177,001548:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.

021263,001634: 25,2351           02001        BIT11+1            OCT      02001                                 
021264,001635: 
021265,001636:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                  R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
021266,001637: 
021267,001638:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021268,001639:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
021269,001640:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
021270,001641:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
021271,001642:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
021272,001643:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
021273,001644:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
021274,001645:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
021275,001646:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
021276,001647:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
021277,001648:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS. IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
021278,001649:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
021279,001650:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
021280,001651:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
021281,001652:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
021282,001653:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
021283,001654:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
021284,001655:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
021285,001656:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
021286,001657:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
021287,001658:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
021288,001659:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
021289,001660:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
021290,001661: 
021291,001662:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021292,001663:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
021293,001664:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
021294,001665:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021295,001666:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
021296,001667: 
021297,001668:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021298,001669:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
021299,001670: 
021300,001671:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021301,001672:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
021302,001673:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
021303,001674: 
021304,001675:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021305,001676:                                                                                                  #     NONE
021306,001677: 
021307,001678:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021308,001679: 
021309,001680:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
021310,001681:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLE ATTITUDE-RETURNS
021311,001682:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)                                                   CAN BE DONE IN PRESENT VEH ATTITUDE.
021312,001683: 
021313,001684: 25,2352           43020        RRDESSM            STQ      CLEAR                                 
021314,001685: 25,2353           01116                                    DESRET                                
021315,001686: 25,2354           00271                                    RRNBSW                                
021316,001687: 25,2355           77624                           CALL                                           #  COMPUTES SINES AND COSINES, ORDER Y Z X
021317,001688: 25,2356           47251                                    CDUTRIG                               
021318,001689: 25,2357           45175                           VLOAD    CALL                                  #  LOAD VECTOR AND CALL TRANSFORMATION
021319,001690: 25,2360           01105                                    RRTARGET                              
021320,001691: 25,2361           47413                                    *SMNB*                                
021321,001692: 
021322,001693: 25,2362           77624                           CALL                                           #  GET RR GIMBAL ANGLES IN PRESENT AND
021323,001694: 25,2363           26105                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.
021324,001695: 25,2364           77776                           EXIT                                           
021325,001696: 
021326,001697: 25,2365           00004                           INHINT

021340,001711: 25,2401           75017                           MASK     SURFFBIT                              #  CHECK IF ON LUNAR SURFACE
021341,001712: 25,2402           00006                           EXTEND

021343,001714: 25,2404           02444                           TC       NODESSM                               #  NOT ON MOON-CALL FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER
021344,001715: 
021345,001716:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
021346,001717: 
021347,001718:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
021348,001719:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
021349,001720:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021350,001721:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
021351,001722:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
021352,001723:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
021353,001724:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
021354,001725:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
021355,001726:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
021356,001727:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
021357,001728:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
021358,001729:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
021359,001730:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
021360,001731:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
021361,001732:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
021362,001733:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED. IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
021363,001734:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
021364,001735:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
021365,001736:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
021366,001737:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
021367,001738:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
021368,001739: 
021369,001740:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021370,001741:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.

021511,001882: 25,2546           03512        20.5DEGS           DEC      .11389                                
021512,001883: 
021513,001884:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
021514,001885: 
021515,001886:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021516,001887:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
021517,001888:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
021518,001889:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
021519,001890:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
021520,001891:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED. IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
021521,001892:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
021522,001893:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
021523,001894:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
021524,001895:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021525,001896:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
021526,001897:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
021527,001898:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
021528,001899:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
021529,001900:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
021530,001901:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
021531,001902:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
021532,001903:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
021533,001904:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
021534,001905:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
021535,001906:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
021536,001907:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
021537,001908:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
021538,001909:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
021539,001910:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
021540,001911:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
021541,001912: 
021542,001913:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021543,001914:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
021544,001915:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
021545,001916:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
021546,001917: 
021547,001918:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021548,001919:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
021549,001920: 
021550,001921:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021551,001922:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
021552,001923: 
021553,001924:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
021554,001925: 
021555,001926:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
021556,001927:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
021557,001928: 
021558,001929:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
021559,001930:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
021560,001931:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
021561,001932: 
021562,001933: 25,2547           41101        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES                              
021563,001934: 
021564,001935: 25,2550           75011                           MASK     REMODBIT

021568,001939: 25,2554           05271        DESLOOP            TC       FIXDELAY                              #  2 SAMPLES PER SECOND.
021569,001940: 25,2555           00062                           DEC      50         B-14

021571,001942: 25,2556           35014        STDESIG            CAF      BIT11                                 
021572,001943: 25,2557           71101                           MASK     RADMODES                              #  SEE IF GIMBAL LIMIT MONITOR HAS FOUND US
021573,001944: 25,2560           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  OUT OF BOUNDS. IF SO, THIS BIT SHOWS A
021574,001945: 25,2561           12613                           TCF      BADDES                                #  REPOSITION TO BE IN PROGRESS.
021575,001946: 
021576,001947: 25,2562           11101                           CCS      RADMODES                              #  SEE IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE WANTED.

021578,001949: 25,2564           12566                           TCF      +2                                    #  LIMITS BUT GO RIGHT TO FINDVAC ENTRY.

021582,001953: 25,2567           75015                           MASK     BIT10                                 #  PROBLEM (DATA GOOD IF LOCK-ON WANTED OR
021583,001954: 25,2570           10000                           CCS      A                                     #  WITHIN LIMITS IF NOT). IF SO, EXIT AFTER
021584,001955: 25,2571           13502                           TCF      ENDRADAR                              #  CHECKING RR CDU FAIL.
