021619,001990: 25,2625           20002        B14+B2             OCT      20002                                 
021620,001991: 
021621,001992:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
021622,001993: 
021623,001994:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
021624,001995:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
021625,001996:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
021626,001997:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
021627,001998:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
021628,001999:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
021629,002000:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
021630,002001:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
021631,002002:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
021632,002003:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
021633,002004:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
021634,002005:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
021635,002006:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
021636,002007:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
021637,002008:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
021638,002009:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
021639,002010:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
021640,002011:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
021641,002012:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
021642,002013:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
021643,002014:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
021644,002015:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
021645,002016:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
021646,002017:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
021647,002018:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
021648,002019:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
021649,002020:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
021650,002021:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
021651,002022:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
021652,002023:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
021653,002024:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
021654,002025:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
021655,002026:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
021656,002027:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
021657,002028:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
021658,002029:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
021659,002030:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
021660,002031:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
021661,002032: 
021662,002033:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
021663,002034:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
021664,002035: 
021665,002036:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
021666,002037:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
021667,002038:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
021668,002039: 
021669,002040:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
021670,002041:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
021671,002042: 
021672,002043:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
021673,002044:                                                                                                  #  NONE
021674,002045: 
021675,002046:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
021676,002047: 
021677,002048:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)

022387,002758:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66

022391,002762:

022393,002764:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR

022418,002789:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
022419,002790:

022619,002990: 
022620,002991:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
022621,002992:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
022622,002993:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
022623,002994: 
022624,002995:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022625,002996: 
022626,002997:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
022627,002998:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
022628,002999:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
022629,003000: 
022630,003001:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022631,003002:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
022632,003003:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
022633,003004:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
022634,003005:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
022635,003006:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
022636,003007:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
022637,003008: 
022638,003009: 
022639,003010:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022640,003011:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
022641,003012:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
022642,003013: 
022643,003014:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022644,003015:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
022645,003016:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
022646,003017:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
022647,003018:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
022648,003019:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
022649,003020: 
022650,003021: 
022651,003022:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022652,003023:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
022653,003024:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
022654,003025:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
022655,003026:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
022656,003027:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
022657,003028:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
022658,003029:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
022659,003030:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
022660,003031:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
022661,003032:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
022662,003033:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
022663,003034:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
022664,003035:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
022665,003036:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG

023016,003387: 26,3133           50554                                    R22LEM93                              
023017,003388:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023018,003389: 
023019,003390:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
023020,003391:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
023021,003392:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
023022,003393: 
023023,003394:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023024,003395:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
023025,003396:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
023026,003397: 
023027,003398:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023028,003399:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
023029,003400:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
023030,003401:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
023031,003402:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
023032,003403:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
023033,003404: 
023034,003405:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023035,003406:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
023036,003407:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
023037,003408:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
023038,003409:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
023039,003410:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
023040,003411:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
023041,003412: 
023042,003413: 26,3134           77624        LSR22.4            CALL                                           
023043,003414: 26,3135           27362                                    INTSTALL                              
023044,003415: 26,3136           43014                           SET      CLEAR                                 
023045,003416: 26,3137           01472                                    STATEFLG                              
023046,003417: 26,3140           01674                                    VINTFLAG                              #  CALL TO GET LM POS + VEL IN REF COORD.
023047,003418: 26,3141           77624                           CALL                                           
023048,003419: 26,3142           55176                                    INTGRCAL                              
023049,003420: 26,3143           77624                           CALL                                           
023050,003421: 26,3144           11054                                    GRP2PC                                
023051,003422: 26,3145           45014                           CLEAR    CALL                                  
023052,003423: 26,3146           02666                                    DMENFLG                               #  SET MATRIX SIZE TO 6X6 FOR INCORP
023053,003424: 26,3147           27362                                    INTSTALL                              
023054,003425: 26,3150           46145                           DLOAD    BHIZ                                  #  IS THIS FIRST TIME THROUGH
023055,003426: 26,3151           03450                                    MARKCTR                               
023056,003427: 26,3152           55165                                    INITWMX6                              #  YES. INITIALIZE 6X6 W-MATRIX
023057,003428: 26,3153           43014                           CLEAR    SET                                   
023058,003429: 26,3154           01675                                    D6OR9FLG                              
023059,003430: 26,3155           01476                                    DIM0FLAG                              
023060,003431: 26,3156           43014                           SET      CLEAR                                 
023061,003432: 26,3157           01474                                    VINTFLAG                              
023062,003433: 26,3160           01673                                    INTYPFLG                              
023063,003434: 26,3161           77624                           CALL                                           
023064,003435: 26,3162           55176                                    INTGRCAL                              
023065,003436: 26,3163           77650                           GOTO                                           
023066,003437: 26,3164           54523                                    RANGEBQ                               
023067,003438: 
023068,003439: 26,3165           77624        INITWMX6           CALL                                           
023069,003440: 26,3166           55205                                    WLINIT                                #  INITIALIZE W-MATRIX
023070,003441: 26,3167           45014                           SET      CALL                                  
023071,003442: 26,3170           01474                                    VINTFLAG                              
023072,003443: 26,3171           26622                                    SETIFLGS

023167,003538: 
023168,003539:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
023169,003540:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC

023224,003595: 26,3362  E7,1433                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023225,003596: 
023226,003597:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
023227,003598:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE  SDC          DATE 1-15-67
023228,003599: 
023229,003600: 
023230,003601:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
023231,003602: 
023232,003603:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
023233,003604:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
023234,003605:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
023235,003606:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
023236,003607: 
023237,003608: 
023238,003609:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
023239,003610: 
023240,003611: 
023241,003612:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
023242,003613: 
023243,003614:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
023244,003615:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
023245,003616:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
023246,003617:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
023247,003618:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
023248,003619: 
023249,003620: 
023250,003621:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -  TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
023251,003622: 
023252,003623: 
023253,003624:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
023254,003625: 
023255,003626:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
023256,003627:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
023257,003628:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
023258,003629: 
023259,003630:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
023260,003631:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
023261,003632:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
023262,003633:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
023263,003634: 
023264,003635:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
023265,003636:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
023266,003637:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
023267,003638:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
023268,003639:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
023269,003640: 
023270,003641: 26,3362                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24
